                  <i>
                   <b>
                    via BettiniPhoto
                   </b>
                  </i>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Stage 19: Just survive
                  <br/>
                  "Today was probably one the most painful and difficult days I have ever had in my cycling career. The injuries and the heat made this last mountain stage of Le Tour de France seem never ending! I couldn't have abandoned though, we are so close to Paris, it wouldn't have been fair to me and the rest of the team. I had to fight. 
 The worst day I've had on the bike for 10 years. Finishing this stage has been more than a victory for me." 
 - Peter Sagan finishes stage 19 within the time cut.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <i>
                   <b>
                    A broken nose for Taylor Phinney gallantly finishing last.
                   </b>
                  </i>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <i>
                   <b>
                    On the menu: Col du Tourmalet (without the lamas).
                   </b>
                  </i>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <i>
                   <b>
                    Pierre LaTour's ride in the best young classification is astounding.
                   </b>
                  </i>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  A look back at 2 great champions:
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <i>
                   <b>
                    Felice Gimondi, stage 17 1969 TdF
                   </b>
                  </i>
